				<script type="text/javascript">
			$J( function() {
				BindAutoFlyoutEvents();

				var $Window = $J(window);
				var $Header = $J('#store_header');
				var $ResponsiveNavWindowShadeCtn = $J('#responsive_store_nav_ctn');
				var $ResponsiveNavOverlay = $J('#responsive_store_nav_overlay');
				var $ResponsiveNavOverlayCtn = $J('#responsive_store_nav_overlay_ctn');
				var $ResponsiveNavOverlayBottom = $J('#responsive_store_nav_overlay_bottom');
				var $HeaderWrapper;
				$Window.on('Responsive_SmallScreenModeToggled.StoreMenu', function() {
					var bUseSmallScreenMode = window.UseSmallScreenMode && window.UseSmallScreenMode();

											if ( !$HeaderWrapper )
							$HeaderWrapper = $Header.wrap( $J('<div/>', {'class': 'responsive_store_nav_ctn_spacer'} ) ).parent();

						if ( bUseSmallScreenMode )
							$ResponsiveNavWindowShadeCtn.append( $Header );
						else
							$HeaderWrapper.append( $Header );


						if ( bUseSmallScreenMode )
						{
							$Header.css( 'visibility', 'hidden' );
							$Header.show();

							var nStartingScrollPosition = $J('#store_header').height();
							if ( $Window.scrollTop() < nStartingScrollPosition )
								$Window.scrollTop( nStartingScrollPosition );

							$Header.css('visibility', 'visible');
						}
									} );
				
				window.setTimeout( function() { $J(window).trigger('Responsive_SmallScreenModeToggled.StoreMenu'); }, 0 );

										var g_rgUserPreferences = {
							excluded_tags : [],
							excluded_content_descriptors : [3,4]						};
						
													g_rgUserPreferences['use_store_query'] = 1;
						
						g_rgUserPreferences['use_search_spellcheck'] = 1;
						g_rgUserPreferences['search_creators_and_tags'] = 1;

						if( $J('#searchform').length > 0 )
						{
							// default search support where the web page includes the search edit control
							EnableSearchSuggestions( $J('#searchform')[0].elements['term'], '1_5_9_', 'SG', 1, 'schinese', g_rgUserPreferences, '20231214' );
						}
						else 
						{
							// search support for the mobile client.  the mobile client has a native search edit control but relies on the web content to perform the query and show results
													}
				
				// make genre categories expand/collapse on mobile
				$J(document).on( 'click', '.popup_genre_expand_header', function ( event ) {
					if ( !UseSmallScreenMode() )
						return;

					event.preventDefault();
					var $Element = $J(this);
					var $Target = $J('.popup_genre_expand_content[data-genre-group=' + $Element.data('genre-group') + ']' );
					if ( $Element.data('group-expanded') )
					{
						$Target.slideUp();
						$Element.data( 'group-expanded', false );
					}
					else
					{
						$Target.slideDown();
						$Element.data( 'group-expanded', true );
					}
				});
			} );
		</script>

                                        <div class="slider" id="highlight_slider">

                                            </div>

                                    <script type="text/javascript">
                                        $J( function() {
                                            var player = new HighlightPlayer( {
                                                elemPlayerArea: 'highlight_player_area',
                                                elemStrip: 'highlight_strip',
                                                elemStripScroll: 'highlight_strip_scroll',
                                                elemSlider: 'highlight_slider',
                                                rgScreenshotURLs: rgScreenshotURLs
                                            } );

                                            $J('#highlight_slider_right').click( function() {
                                                player.Transition( true );
                                            });
                                            $J('#highlight_slider_left').click( function() {
                                                player.TransitionBack( true );
                                            });

                                            
                                                // swipe gesture handling for the media carousel

                                                // TODO: We may want to move all of this to the player class so it has built in touch gesture support.
                                                // First testing here as part of new mobile ux.

                                                var k_nElementWidth = 120;
                                                var k_playerItemClassName = '.highlight_player_item';
                                                var g_nStripWidth = 1080;
                                                var g_nMediaItems = player.m_elemPlayerArea.find( '.highlight_player_item' ).length;
                                                var g_TouchEventStart = null;

                                                // Handle left/right swipe on the media playback by moving forward or backward when the swipe completes
                                                $J('#highlight_player_area').on("touchstart", function (event) {
                                                    g_TouchEventStart = event;
                                                });
                                                $J('#highlight_player_area').on("touchmove", function (event) {

                                                    if ( typeof g_TouchEventStart == undefined )
                                                        return;

                                                    var xdiff = Math.abs( g_TouchEventStart.originalEvent.changedTouches[0].screenX - event.originalEvent.changedTouches[0].screenX );
                                                    var ydiff = Math.abs( g_TouchEventStart.originalEvent.changedTouches[0].screenY - event.originalEvent.changedTouches[0].screenY );

                                                    // To reduce unintended page scroll during a horizontal swipe block the default handler when it looks like the user
                                                    // is in the process of performaing a horizontal scroll
                                                    if ( xdiff > ydiff && ( typeof event.cancelable !== 'boolean' || event.cancelable ) )
                                                        event.preventDefault();

                                                });
                                                $J('#highlight_player_area').on("touchend", function (eventEnd) {

                                                    if ( typeof g_TouchEventStart.originalEvent.changedTouches[0] == undefined ||
                                                        typeof eventEnd.originalEvent.changedTouches[0] == undefined )
                                                        return;

                                                    var xdiff = g_TouchEventStart.originalEvent.changedTouches[0].screenX - eventEnd.originalEvent.changedTouches[0].screenX;
                                                    var ydiff = g_TouchEventStart.originalEvent.changedTouches[0].screenY - eventEnd.originalEvent.changedTouches[0].screenY;

                                                    // clear out the touch start event
                                                    g_TouchEventStart = null;

                                                    // ignore the swipe if it was short and could've been intended as a tap, or the
                                                    // direction was more vertical than horizontal
                                                    if ( Math.abs( xdiff ) < 20 || Math.abs( ydiff ) > Math.abs( xdiff ) )
                                                        return;

                                                    // we're handling this event
                                                    if ( typeof event.cancelable !== 'boolean' || event.cancelable )
                                                        event.preventDefault();

                                                    // move forward or backward but don't wrap as that would be a jarring user experience
                                                    if ( xdiff > 0 )
                                                    {
                                                        var $NextItem = player.m_activeItem.next( k_playerItemClassName );
                                                        if ( $NextItem.length )
                                                            player.Transition( true );
                                                    }
                                                    else
                                                    {
                                                        var $NextItem = player.m_activeItem.prev( k_playerItemClassName );
                                                        if ( $NextItem.length )
                                                            player.TransitionBack( true );
                                                    }
                                                });

                                                // when the thumbnail strip is swiped move the strip at a granular level
                                                // so it feels active.  The active image does not update because when testing the code to
                                                // make it change the active element it seemed annoying
                                                var g_nSwipeStartingPosition = 0;
                                                var g_nMaxScroll = g_nMediaItems > 3 ? ( ( g_nMediaItems - 3 ) * k_nElementWidth ) : 0;

                                                $J('#highlight_strip_scroll').on("touchstart", function (event) {
                                                    g_TouchEventStart = event;
                                                    g_nSwipeStartingPosition = parseInt( player.m_elemStripScroll.css( 'left' ) );

                                                    player.StopCycle();
                                                });
                                                $J('#highlight_strip_scroll').on("touchmove", function (event) {

                                                    if ( typeof g_TouchEventStart == undefined )
                                                        return;

                                                    // To reduce unintended page scroll during a horizontal swipe block the default handler when it looks like the user
                                                    // is in the process of performaing a horizontal scroll
                                                    var xdiff = parseInt( event.originalEvent.changedTouches[0].screenX - g_TouchEventStart.originalEvent.changedTouches[0].screenX );
                                                    var ydiff = parseInt( event.originalEvent.changedTouches[0].screenY - g_TouchEventStart.originalEvent.changedTouches[0].screenY );
                                                    if ( Math.abs(ydiff) > Math.abs(xdiff) )
                                                        return;

                                                    // move the scroll strip without changing the selected item
                                                    var nNewScrollPosition = parseInt( g_nSwipeStartingPosition + xdiff );

                                                    // check that we don't scroll past the ends
                                                    if ( nNewScrollPosition > 0 )
                                                        nNewScrollPosition = 0;
                                                    else if ( nNewScrollPosition < (-1 * g_nMaxScroll) )
                                                        nNewScrollPosition = (-1 * g_nMaxScroll);

                                                    // set the new scroll position
                                                    player.m_elemStripScroll.css( 'left', nNewScrollPosition + 'px' );

                                                    // we're handling this event
                                                    if ( typeof event.cancelable !== 'boolean' || event.cancelable )
                                                        event.preventDefault();
                                                });
                                                $J('#highlight_strip_scroll').on("touchend", function (eventEnd) {
                                                    g_TouchEventStart = null;
                                                    g_nSwipeStartingPosition = 0;
                                                });

										
                                            if( window.location.hash )
                                            {
                                                var ssid = window.location.hash.substr(1);
                                                player.HighlightScreenshot(ssid);
                                            }
                                        } );
                                    </script>
                                                            </div>
                        					</div>
				</div>
				<div style="clear: both;"></div>
			</div>
			</div>

																			<h1>为何要采用抢先体验这种模式？</h1>
										“Early Access allows us to reach those early adopters who want to experience the latest in Ghosts of Tabor and support a game that is in rapid development. Join our discord to get involved: <a href="https://steamcommunity.com/linkfilter/?url=https://discord.gg/ghostsoftabor" target="_blank" rel=" noopener">https://discord.gg/ghostsoftabor</a>”

										<h1>这款游戏的抢先体验状态大约持续多久？</h1>
										“We plan on staying in EA until all major features are implemented, including the ones the community thinks are crucial.”

										<h1>计划中的完整版本和抢先体验版本到底有多少不同？</h1>
										“The full version is planned to include many more maps, gameplay features, and improvements that are currently not present in the Early Access version.”

										<h1>抢先体验版本的现状如何？</h1>
										“Ghosts of Tabor is the only extraction based VR FPS PvPvE survival game<br>
where you will have to use your wits, skills and resources to survive. Inspired by games<br>
such as Escape from Tarkov and Day Z, the game features a variety of scenarios from<br>
scavenging, looting to crafting. Make your safehouse your own by building your<br>
personal collection weapons and gear to display in your armory.<br>
Ghosts of Tabor is packed with features for unlimited replayability including:<br>
<br>
● Simultaneous PVP and PVE - Avoid both players and armed AI<br>
● Scavenge for a wide variety of loot such as gear, weapons, attachments, ammo,<br>
medical, food and water<br>
● Squad up or go at it alone in the world's most dangerous looting grounds<br>
● Make your way to your extraction point to get out with your life and your gear.<br>
● Customize weapons and craft items<br>
● Craft ammo of different types and sizes<br>
● Variety of weapons ranging from handguns to assault rifles<br>
● Huge armory to display your arsenal of weapons, armor, and gear<br>
● Choose your load out carefully<br>
● Visit the marketplace to source anything you may need for your next raid<br>
● Complete missions with vendors to unlock special goods<br>
<br>
Choose your playstyle from guns-a- blazing or take a stealthy approach. It’s up to you to<br>
find a way to escape Tabor alive. Can you survive the Ghosts of Tabor?”

										<h1>在抢先体验期间和结束之后，游戏价格会有所不同吗？</h1>

							<h2>关于这款游戏</h2>
							<h2 class="bb_tag"><strong>SURVIVE &amp; STAY ALIVE</strong></h2>Survival systems like health/hunger/thirst and needing to eat/heal to stay alive.<br><img src="https://cdn.akamai.steamstatic.com/steam/apps/1957780/extras/survive1.gif?t=1693412431"><h2 class="bb_tag"><strong>EXPLORE, LOOT &amp; SHOOT</strong></h2>Large maps that allow for multiplayer exploration, looting, intense shoot-outs, snipers.<br><img src="https://cdn.akamai.steamstatic.com/steam/apps/1957780/extras/shoot2.gif?t=1693412431"><h2 class="bb_tag"><strong>UPGRADE YOUR ARSENAL</strong></h2>Trading with vendors AI and P2P to attain better gear, make money, and craft equipment.<br><img src="https://cdn.akamai.steamstatic.com/steam/apps/1957780/extras/arsenal2.gif?t=1693412431"><h2 class="bb_tag">AMAZING ENVIRONMENTS</h2>Experience amazing VR maps like Island of Tabor and Missile Silo at Closed Beta Launch.<br><img src="https://cdn.akamai.steamstatic.com/steam/apps/1957780/extras/maps5.gif?t=1693412431"><br><br>Ghosts of Tabor is the only extraction based VR FPS PvPvE survival game<br>where you will have to use your wits, skills and resources to survive. Inspired by games<br>such as Escape from Tarkov and Day Z, the game features a variety of scenarios from<br>scavenging, looting to crafting. Make your safehouse your own by building your<br>personal collection weapons and gear to display in your armory.<br>Ghosts of Tabor is packed with features for unlimited replayability including:<br>● Simultaneous PVP and PVE - Avoid both players and armed AI<br>● Scavenge for a wide variety of loot such as gear, weapons, attachments, ammo,<br>medical, food and water<br>● Squad up or go at it alone in the world's most dangerous looting grounds<br>● Make your way to your extraction point to get out with your life and your gear.<br>● Customize weapons and craft items<br>● Craft ammo of different types and sizes<br>● Variety of weapons ranging from handguns to assault rifles<br>● Huge armory to display your arsenal of weapons, armor, and gear<br>● Choose your load out carefully<br>● Visit the marketplace to source anything you may need for your next raid<br>● Complete missions with vendors to unlock special goods<br>Choose your playstyle from guns-a- blazing or take a stealthy approach. It’s up to you to<br>find a way to escape Tabor alive. Can you survive the Ghosts of Tabor?						</div>

									<div class="early_access_review tooltip" data-tooltip-text="该评测被撰写时，Ghosts of Tabor 被标记为 Steam 抢先体验游戏">抢先体验版本评测</div>
				
													<div class="responsive_review_leftcol_ctn" id="ReviewContentsummary135417093_leftcol_ctn"></div>
				
				<div class="postedDate">
					发布于：3 月 26 日																					<div class="responsive_purchase_source">
															Steam 直接购买													</div>
									</div>

								
				<div class="content">
					3月26日感受：好游戏，更新勤快，玩着快乐，没有作弊者，推荐。已知bug：手枪放进背包里时，即使背包不变红手枪也没法固定在包里，必须不断尝试一个特定的角度和未知；如果在仓库里拔出手枪弹匣，不论剩余多少子弹都会变成1颗或更少，插进去再拔出来就1颗不剩，即使用装弹机装满子弹，上述问题还是会发生；如果胸口挂了主武器，不管是开门、开箱，还是下梯子都会抓住枪，已经发生2次想下梯子结果抓住了枪没抓住梯子的情况，直接摔死；子弹击中硬物体表面会产生“打水漂”一样的的反弹，一颗子弹反弹后会留一连串弹孔，有5个甚至更多。建议：增加背包存放手枪的栏位；修复拔出弹夹会使弹匣内子弹数量变为1或更少的问题；将主武器位置改为右肩；增加将枪连接到指定槽位的功能，让武器脱手后能像栓了绳子一样自动回到槽位；增加查看剩余子弹数量的功能；增加显示物品名称的功能；增加弹匣回收袋，方便存放换下来的弹匣；让玩家能一次拾取更多子弹，否则向弹匣里一颗一颗塞子弹太难了；增加霰弹槽位，否则霰弹枪只能变成摆设。最后，请制作组好好玩玩<b> Hot Dogs, Horseshoes &amp; Hand Grenades </b>，尤其要安装几个经典mod，请认真学习他们的游戏功能，改善这款游戏。希望越做越好！					<div class="gradient"></div>
				</div>

				<div class="posted">

								<div class="num_owned_games"><a href="https://steamcommunity.com/id/Bucoid/games/?tab=all">帐户内拥有 99 项产品</a></div>
												<div class="num_reviews"><a href="https://steamcommunity.com/id/Bucoid/recommended/">14 篇评测</a></div>

			<div class="rightcol" id="ReviewContentsummary138435034_rightcol">
								<a href="https://steamcommunity.com/id/Bucoid/recommended/1957780/" class="vote_header tooltip" data-tooltip-text="阅读完整评测">
					<div class="thumb">
						<img id="votingImage" src="https://store.akamai.steamstatic.com/public/shared/images/userreviews/icon_thumbsDown_v6.png" width="40" height="40">

										<img class="review_source tooltip" data-tooltip-text="产品是从 Steam 直接购买的" src="https://store.akamai.steamstatic.com/public/shared/images/userreviews/icon_review_steam.png">
					
					<div class="title ellipsis">不推荐</div>
										<div class="hours ellipsis">
						总时数 21.3 小时												（评测时 15.7 小时）											</div>
									</a>
				
									<div class="early_access_review tooltip" data-tooltip-text="该评测被撰写时，Ghosts of Tabor 被标记为 Steam 抢先体验游戏">抢先体验版本评测</div>
				
													<div class="responsive_review_leftcol_ctn" id="ReviewContentsummary138435034_leftcol_ctn"></div>
				
				<div class="postedDate">
					发布于：5 月 17 日																					<div class="responsive_purchase_source">
															Steam 直接购买													</div>
									</div>

								
				<div class="content">
					首先，开门见山的说下，这款游戏确实是类塔科夫或者说，他就是你想象中的那个游戏的VR化<br>（还原了高难度和定时删档和咕咕咕更新，还有挂，对的这游戏也有孤儿开挂）<br>至于为什么我是不推荐这款游戏的呢<br>其实很简单，有很多方面的原因<br><br>第一，随机bug和多设备兼容性奇差无比<br>我在我的5800H+3070的笔记本上使用quest2自带的link根本没办法运行这款游戏<br>不管是在游戏提供的openXR或者说OC模式或者是steamvr模式下都会出现致命的bug<br>只要我一互动物品（拿弹匣，开门，或者搜刮物质）都会闪退且无法恢复<br>我尝试过非常多的方法，包括但不限于更新显卡驱动，限制显卡频率，重下游戏，重新设置oculus，使用openxr，oculus，steamvr等方法启动本游戏，均会复现上面的互动bug然后闪退<br>然后我用了我的第二台设备尝试运行这款游戏，5600+2080ti<br>不出我所料还是复现了上面的问题，用oc模式下进游戏100%互动闪退，且无法恢复<br>我尝试了很多次都没办法解决，后面我甚至把我最老的VR设备，oculus rift cv1拿出来运行这款游戏<br>你猜猜怎么样，它好了，它不会闪退了，我不管是互动弹匣还是开门搜刮，还是运行都一切正常了<br>至于后面我用quest2怎么正常运行这款游戏.....<br>卸载steamvr用游戏自带的第三个选项的steamvr模式启动本游戏，虽然进游戏是cv1的手柄位置，但是确实不会闪退了<br>也算是在quest2上正常运行了？？？<br>不，当我以为我解决问题后尝试在5800H+3070的笔记本上使用这种奇怪的方式运行游戏的时候，它还是不起作用<br>我放弃了，后面均使用5600+2080ti的设备运行这款游戏，这个问题直接决定你是否能运行游戏，所以我是不推荐这款游戏的，当然了不止这一个方面，后面还有<br><br>第二，游戏的bug以及多方面的不足，作为一个抢先体验的游戏有bug太正常不过了，但是这游戏的bug是有影响正常游戏的，所以说要提一嘴，未知原因闪退的bug，这个触发的概率是非常高的，可能会在任何无原因的情况下游戏闪退，而且无法重连回战局，加上这游戏目前没有投保系统你闪退了你的装备就会遁入虚空消失，这个有多么恶心呢，1是这个闪退bug触发概率非常高，2就是这游戏没有重连机制导致你身上一身十几万的装备，闪退了直接没了，这游戏目前的经济系统和塔科夫1格1w不太一样，不是随便摸一背包垃圾就能起套全装，你塞满整个背包的物资大概率是不如你身上那套全装的，会很让人头疼（这也影响目前游戏的玩法）<br><br>第三，任务系统的不合理性，首先我们先不吐槽塔科夫的物价和这游戏的物价，先单说下任务系统吧，大伙可能都玩过塔科夫，知道塔科夫的任务一直是那样的一条线，青铜怀表啥的，标油罐车，埋火药，标救护车，上交医疗包啥的，目前这游戏只有少量提交任务没有任务线（但是目前有任务场景，比如博物馆内某房间有个scav尸体和一把枪，可能是某个商人的线人），这游戏目前有的任务主要只有一种，击杀任务<br>可能你不太理解击杀任务是个啥，简单说下吧，塔科夫的风波做过吧，手枪杀pmc啥的，还有塔科夫神射手啥的天神射手，大家都很清楚，这种任务做起来有多么痛苦，而目前游戏中只有这种击杀任务，而且是重复接的击杀任务<br>1级商人到2级商人需要2.5w的信任度，而击杀12个scav或者击杀15个scav用步枪的任务你猜猜给多少好感，1-3k左右，你要升级1级商人到2级你需要重复完成这种任务很多次，而目前这游戏一局内的scav数量很少，只要你不去博物馆或者去军事基地击杀哨塔ai和巡逻ai，那么你一局就只能遇见几个scav，有人会说：既然军事基地和博物馆的scav多，你为什么不去呢<br>这又要提到这游戏另一些的击杀任务了，上面说了，1级到2级商人要2.5w好感，但是击杀几十个scav就只给几K的好感度，要杀上百个sacv才能升级，而这游戏里面还有另一类的任务，击杀PMC的任务<br>这些任务因为是击杀玩家所以说给的好感极高，几乎1-2个PMC的人头就相当于你去跑几局杀完的15个sacv的好感，所以说为了快速做任务，击杀pmc是首选<br>对，因为目前任务线的不完整只有击杀任务，如果你是个新入坑的萌新，1级商店只有一把破sks和一些手枪冲锋枪可以买，想去杀点sacv提升商人等级然后循序渐进，那么在你开枪的第一秒，几乎全地图都会听见你的枪声知道你的位置<br>有人会说，这有什么，开枪暴露自己不是很正常的吗<br>对，你忘了这游戏升级商人只能通过重复接击杀任务才能提升吗，杀PMC是提升最快的方法，所以说如果你想要杀点sacv然后搜点东西就撤离下一把快乐游戏？<br>不不不，只要你开枪暴露了自己，不到2分钟内，马上你就会知道什么叫做死亡，马上就会有接了击杀pmc任务的全装（阿尔金俄重弹鼓消音M4或者AK带着5.56AP 7.62AP来找你）<br>你能理解一把破机瞄枪面对全装的无力感吗，打在别人甲上都不掉血，当然了，你如果枪法好，遇见没带头盔的玩家一枪头干死了，你也可以舔走别人的装备肥肥撤离，但还是那句话，只要你开枪了，全图的全装玩家都会来找你，你想要靠击杀几百个sacv提升商人等级几乎是走不通的（杀十几个scav给几k的好感度，1-2级商人2.5w，2-3级7.5w，你得杀几百个scav都提升不了1级），目前游戏任务树的不完善导致你入坑的体验会非常非常非常非常差<br>有多差我不好说，反正你相信我，当你做了一次击杀sacv的任务就给了1-2k的好感度，然后看着1-2要2.5w的好感度的时候，你不会想继续玩下去的，因为这游戏目前的内容度不够，导致几乎只有PVP一条路可走，而且因为没有投保和保险箱你进图只要一旦死亡就是纯亏，加上时不时的闪退，导致你玩了一天卢布也不会变多，商人的好感度任务进度也不会变多，简单的说就是纯拖玩家进度，加上也没scav和投保，萌新入坑难度比塔科夫白边档末还难很多<br>目前本游戏有很多问题，如果你真的很喜欢或者想要体验下，买个白边试试，相信我你很快就会退出来怀疑人生的，为什么要来游戏里上班，当然了，如果你真的很喜欢玩这款游戏，也可以来本游戏的摸鱼群：797551816找点萌新自强队（<br><br>目前制作组有很多想法，军事基地旁边的尸坑，撤离点附近的地雷和锁着的地下设施，博物馆的大量scav聚集和死在博物馆某房间内的scav线人，但是这些统统都没办法在目前的版本体验到，目前游戏完全只是个demo，枪械手感奇差无比（居然还有VR游戏有归零bug，瞄具不如激光有用）<br>我希望游戏制作组会把游戏改的很好，包括但不限于上线跳蚤市场，scav模式，投保系统，商人对应的任务故事线以及新地图（目前地图内有城区和海岸线区，目前开放的地图为海岛地图，非城市内，虽然这款游戏未来可期，但是我真的只能在目前这个版本给个不推荐，其中包括很多原因。<br>					<div class="gradient"></div>
				</div>

				<div class="content">
					测试第一天就开始玩了，从最开始的灾难级游玩到现在，总结一个个人的看法：游戏框架好，做的不错，VR版塔科夫，但目前还有BUG,官方勤奋点，BUG修复，不断更新， 将会是VR爆款联机FPS对战捡垃圾游戏，希望制作组不要摆烂，前景无限。<br><br><br>更新评测：发售到2023年3月31日，10天时间，已经修复了很多BUG,就像VD作者说的这游戏的开发商很勤奋，从最开始的褒贬不一到现在的特别好评，游戏模式、内容占一头、制作组的努力和勤奋也占一头，希望继续保持下去，定期更新，边修边更，大家都很爱玩这游戏。					<div class="gradient"></div>
